The feedback speed is highly recognized and the work is reliable. The restaurant's meals are also extremely rich, mainly river food, including Guangxi cuisine and Thai cuisine. The white-cut chicken, snail duck feet stew, and lemon duck are all very good and worth recommending. You can also eat sea cucumbers and fish maws for breakfast, and seasonal fruits are also very appetizing. If you are traveling with your family, you can stay in the hotel for a day, swim, ride a bicycle, feed the tortoises, and make a frisbee in the afternoon and play on the grass. msg:When I chose the hotel two months ago, I was yearning for the beauty of Zaiye. After I actually checked in, I realized that the beauty of Zaiye is everywhere. The unforgettable photography works, the green fans and purple flowers of banana trees, the sparkling waves of the Black Water River, the fiery red of kapok flowers against the pale green of distant mountains, the roof of the mushroom house and the little mushroom on the lawn...
Every staff member of Zaiye has a smile from the heart, and every greeting and every care makes us feel like spring breeze. It can be said that the professional and friendly service of the staff of Zaiye makes Zaiye present the most perfect side!
It must be mentioned that the food in Zaiye is also remarkable: at almost 5 o'clock in the afternoon, we can still enjoy the beautiful scenery in the lobby as requested, while enjoying the afternoon tea of â€‹â€‹matcha cake, various fruits, and delicious nuts; the next day when we went out, the staff sent the afternoon tea to the room and put the cakes and fruits in the refrigerator attentively; the white fungus and red dates soup in the evening is sweet and soft; the semi-self-service breakfast of sea cucumber, abalone and fish maw is very nourishing, and the wontons with noodles are unique, which is very satisfying!
The weather was also very helpful. The most amazing thing was that after we drove into Zaiye, the gloomy weather began to clear up, and then there were blue skies, white clouds, green trees and red flowers. I was in a great mood! I watched the sunset with my family by the Blackwater River outside the restaurant. Thanks to Zaiye, the time we spent together quietly watching the sunset will always be engraved in our memories...

name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Duplex Family Room - 2-Bedroom
info:Stayed in January 2024
info:Family
info:9 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted January 28, 2024
msg:I had heard from friends that Chongzuo is a very suitable place for rest and the scenery is also beautiful. This time, I took my child and set off immediately at the beginning of the winter vacation.
It was also recommended by a friend to choose Yebai. First of all, the service was very good. They took the initiative to contact and add WeChat and set up a housekeeper group very early, and sent some introductions to the homestay and surrounding attractions for reference.
On the day of check-in, I saw it on the spot and learned more about this area. It is a collection of four homestays by the Black Water River, so it is called "Zaiye Su Ji". Each homestay has about 10 rooms. All the homestay lobbies can be visited. Each has its own characteristics. There is a restaurant, a bar, an outdoor barbecue camping area and a college. Basically, they can be reached on foot. Of course, there are cars for pick-up.
The room type I chose was mainly because there is a slide in the suite. Hahahaha, the child is also very happy to go up and down. The design of the room definitely took a lot of thought. It is very meticulous and thoughtful under the wild luxury style. In addition to the common high-quality hotel supplies, minibar, afternoon tea, snacks, etc., there are also makeup remover towels and disposable bath bags, which are too appropriate.
The staff are all handsome boys and girls. Seeing that I brought my baby, they took the initiative to arrange a DIY hand-painted frisbee for the baby and brought many board games for us to choose from. We also fully experienced the movies and cocktails in the evening. Finally, I have to say that the food in the wild restaurant is really delicious. The breakfast set is very rich. It is best to book the dishes in advance for lunch and dinner because it is not very convenient to purchase. I haven't eaten much Guangxi cuisine before. After eating this restaurant, I deeply enjoyed the beer fish and braised pork hahahaha~
